Kubernetes controller manager is a daemon that embeds\n   110→the core control loops shipped with Kubernetes. In applications of robotics and\n   111→automation, a control loop is a non-terminating loop that regulates the state of\n   112→the system. In Kubernetes, a controller is a control loop that watches the shared\n   113→state of the cluster through the apiserver and makes changes attempting to move the\n   114→current state towards the desired state. Examples of controllers that ship with\n   115→Kubernetes today are the replication controller, endpoints controller, namespace\n   116→controller, and serviceaccounts controller.`,\n   117→\t\tPersistentPreRunE: func(*cobra.Command, []string) error {\n   118→\t\t\t// silence client-go warnings.\n   119→\t\t\t// kube-controller-manager generically watches APIs (including deprecated ones),\n   120→\t\t\t// and CI ensures it works properly against matching kube-apiserver versions.\n   121→\t\t\trestclient.SetDefaultWarningHandler(restclient.NoWarnings{})\n   122→\t\t\t// makes sure feature gates are set before RunE.\n   123→\t\t\treturn s.ComponentGlobalsRegistry.Set()\n   124→\t\t},\n   125→\t\tRunE: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {\n   126→\t\t\tverflag.PrintAndExitIfRequested()\n   127→\n   128→\t\t\t// Activate logging as soon as possible, after that\n   129→\t\t\t// show flags with the final logging configuration.\n 153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\tfs := cmd.Flags()\n   156→\tnamedFlagSets := s.Flags(KnownControllers(), ControllersDisabledByDefault(), ControllerAliases())\n 179→// Run runs the KubeControllerManagerOptions.\n   180→func Run(ctx context.Context, c *config.CompletedConfig) error {\n   181→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   182→\tstopCh := ctx.Done()\n   183→\n   184→\t// To help debugging, immediately log version\n   185→\tlogger.Info(\"Starting\", \"version\", utilversion.Get())\n   186→\n   187→\tlogger.Info(\"Golang settings\", \"GOGC\", 216→\t\thandler := genericcontrollermanager.BuildHandlerChain(unsecuredMux, &c.Authorization, &c.Authentication)\n   217→\t\t// TODO: handle stoppedCh and listenerStoppedCh returned by 249→\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n   250→\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n   251→\t\treturn nil\n   252→\t}\n   253→\n   254→\tid, *leadermigration.LeaderMigrator = nil\n   264→\n   265→\t// If leader migration is enabled, create the LeaderMigrator and prepare for migration\n   266→\tif 276→\t\t//  the controller.\n   277→\t\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor.initFunc = func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n   278→\t\t\tdefer close(leaderMigrator.MigrationReady)\n   279→\t\t\treturn startSATokenControllerInit(ctx, controllerContext, controllerName)\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t}\n   282→\n   283→\tif 289→\t\tif err != nil {\n   290→\t\t\treturn err\n   291→\t\t}\n   292→\n   293→\t\t// Start lease candidate controller for coordinated leader election\n   294→\t\tleaseCandidate, waitForSync, err := 315→\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n   316→\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n   317→\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n   318→\t\t\t\tif 339→\t\t<-leaderMigrator.MigrationReady\n   340→\n   341→\t\t// Start the migration lock.\n   342→\t\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n   343→\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.ResourceLock,\n   344→\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.LeaderName,\n   345→\t\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n   346→\t\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n   347→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting migrated controllers.\")\n   348→\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := 350→\t\t\t\t\t// DO NOT start saTokenController under migration lock\n   351→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(controllerDescriptors, names.ServiceAccountTokenController)\n   352→\t\t\t\t\trun(ctx, ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\n   366→type ControllerContext struct {\n   367→\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n   368→\tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n   369→\n   370→\t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n   371→\tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n   372→\n   373→\t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n   374→\t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n   375→\t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n   376→\t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n   377→\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n   378→\n   379→\t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n   380→\tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n   381→\n   382→\t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n   383→\t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n   384→\t// requested.\n   385→\tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n   386→\n   387→\t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n   388→\t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n   389→\tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n   390→\n   391→\t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n   392→\t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n   393→\t// with list requests simultaneously.\n   394→\tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n   395→\n   396→\t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n   397→\tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n   398→\n   399→\t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n   400→\tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n   401→}\n   402→\n   403→// IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\n   404→func (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n   405→\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n   406→\tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n   407→\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n   408→\t}\n   409→\treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n   410→}\n   411→\n   412→// InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n   413→// that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n   414→// can support the requested features.\n   415→// The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n   416→// that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n   417→// Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n   418→// The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\n   419→type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n   420→\n   421→type ControllerDescriptor struct {\n   422→\tname                      string\n   423→\tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n   424→\trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n   425→\taliases                   []string\n   426→\tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n   427→\tisCloudProviderController bool\n   428→\trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n   429→}\n   430→\n   431→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n   432→\treturn r.name\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n   436→\treturn r.initFunc\n   437→}\n   438→\n   439→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n   440→\treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n   441→}\n   442→\n   443→// GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n   444→// Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\n   445→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n   446→\treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n   447→}\n   448→\n   449→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n   450→\treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n   451→}\n   452→\n   453→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsCloudProviderController() bool {\n   454→\treturn r.isCloudProviderController\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→// RequiresSpecialHandling should return true only in a special non-generic controllers like ServiceAccountTokenController\n   458→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) RequiresSpecialHandling() bool {\n   459→\treturn r.requiresSpecialHandling\n   460→}\n   461→\n   462→// KnownControllers returns all known controllers's name\n   463→func KnownControllers() []string {\n   464→\treturn sets.StringKeySet(NewControllerDescriptors()).List()\n   465→}\n   466→\n   467→// ControllerAliases returns a mapping of aliases to canonical controller names\n   468→func ControllerAliases() map[string]string {\n   469→\taliases := map[string]string{}\n   470→\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n   471→\t\tfor _, alias := range c.GetAliases() {\n   472→\t\t\taliases[alias] = name\n   473→\t\t}\n   474→\t}\n   475→\treturn aliases\n   476→}\n   477→\n   478→func ControllersDisabledByDefault() []string {\n   479→\tvar controllersDisabledByDefault []string\n   480→\n   481→\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n   482→\t\tif c.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n   483→\t\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault = append(controllersDisabledByDefault, name)\n   484→\t\t}\n   485→\t}\n   486→\n   487→\tsort.Strings(controllersDisabledByDefault)\n   488→\n   489→\treturn controllersDisabledByDefault\n   490→}\n   491→\n   492→// NewControllerDescriptors is a public map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n   493→// paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n   494→// This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\n   495→func NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n   496→\tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n   497→\taliases := sets.NewString()\n   498→\n   499→\t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n   500→\tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n   501→\t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n   502→\t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n   503→\t\t}\n   504→\t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n   505→\t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n   506→\t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n   507→\t\t}\n   508→\t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n   509→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n   512→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n   513→\t\t}\n   514→\n   515→\t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n   516→\t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n   517→\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n   518→\t\t\t}\n   519→\t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\n   522→\t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n   523→\t}\n   524→\n   525→\t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. These controllers cannot be initialized\n   526→\t// in the main controller loop initialization, so we add them here only for the metadata and duplication detection.\n   527→\t// app.ControllerDescriptor#RequiresSpecialHandling should return true for such controllers\n   528→\t// The only known special case is the ServiceAccountTokenController which *must* be started\n   529→\t// first to ensure that the SA tokens for future controllers will exist. Think very carefully before adding new\n   530→\t// special controllers.\n   531→\tregister(newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(nil))\n   532→\n   533→\tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n   534→\tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n   535→\tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n   536→\tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n   537→\tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   538→\tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n   539→\tregister(newNamespaceControllerDescriptor())\n   540→\tregister(newServiceAccountControllerDescriptor())\n   541→\tregister(newGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   542→\tregister(newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor())\n   543→\tregister(newJobControllerDescriptor())\n   544→\tregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\n   545→\tregister(newReplicaSetControllerDescriptor())\n   546→\tregister(newHorizontalPodAutoscalerControllerDescriptor())\n   547→\tregister(newDisruptionControllerDescriptor())\n   548→\tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n   549→\tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n   550→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n   551→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestApprovingControllerDescriptor())\n   552→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   553→\tregister(newTTLControllerDescriptor())\n   554→\tregister(newBootstrapSignerControllerDescriptor())\n   555→\tregister(newTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   556→\tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n   557→\tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n   558→\n   559→\tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   560→\tregister(newNodeRouteControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   561→\tregister(newCloudNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor()) // cloud provider controller\n   562→\t// TODO: persistent volume controllers into the IncludeCloudLoops only set as a cloud provider controller.\n   563→\n   564→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeBinderControllerDescriptor())\n   565→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeAttachDetachControllerDescriptor())\n   566→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeExpanderControllerDescriptor())\n   567→\tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n   568→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   569→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   570→\tregister(newVolumeAttributesClassProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   571→\tregister(newTTLAfterFinishedControllerDescriptor())\n   572→\tregister(newRootCACertificatePublisherControllerDescriptor())\n   573→\tregister(newKubeAPIServerSignerClusterTrustBundledPublisherDescriptor())\n   574→\tregister(newEphemeralVolumeControllerDescriptor())\n   575→\n   576→\t// feature gated\n   577→\tregister(newStorageVersionGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   578→\tregister(newResourceClaimControllerDescriptor())\n   579→\tregister(newLegacyServiceAccountTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   580→\tregister(newValidatingAdmissionPolicyStatusControllerDescriptor())\n clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n   599→\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n   600→\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n   601→\t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n   602→\t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n   603→\t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n   604→\t\t\t}\n 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n   619→\t}\n   620→\n   621→\t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n   622→\tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n   623→\tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n   624→\trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n   625→\tgo wait.Until(func() {\n   626→\t\trestMapper.Reset()\n   627→\t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n   628→\n   629→\tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n   630→\t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n   631→\t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n   632→\t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n   633→\t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n   634→\t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n   635→\t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n   636→\t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n   637→\t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n   638→\t}\n   639→\n   640→\tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector specified ControllerContext\n   662→func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n   663→\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n   664→\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n   665→\n   666→\t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n   667→\t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n   668→\tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n   669→\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n   670→\t\tif err != nil {\n   671→\t\t\treturn err\n   672→\t\t}\n   673→\t\tif check != nil {\n   674→\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n   675→\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n   676→\t\t}\n   677→\t}\n   678→\n   679→\t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n   680→\t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n   681→\t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n   682→\t//\n   683→\t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n   684→\t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n   685→\t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n   686→\t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n   687→\t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n   688→\tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n   689→\t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n   690→\t\t\tcontinue\n   691→\t\t}\n   692→\n   693→\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n   694→\t\tif err != nil {\n   695→\t\t\treturn err\n   696→\t\t}\n   697→\t\tif check != nil {\n   698→\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n   699→\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n   700→\t\t}\n   701→\t}\n   702→\n   703→\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n   704→\n   705→\treturn nil\n   706→}\n   707→\n   708→// StartController starts a controller with a specified ControllerContext\n   709→// and performs required pre- and post- checks/actions\n   710→func StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n   711→\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n   712→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   713→\tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n   714→\n   715→\tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n   716→\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) {\n   717→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Controller is disabled by a feature gate\", \"controller\", controllerName, \"requiredFeatureGates\", controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates())\n   718→\t\t\treturn nil, nil\n   719→\t\t}\n   720→\t}\n   721→\n   722→\tif controllerDescriptor.IsCloudProviderController() {\n   723→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping a cloud provider controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   724→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   725→\t}\n   726→\n   727→\tif !controllerCtx.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor) {\n   728→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: controller is disabled\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   729→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   730→\t}\n   731→\n   732→\ttime.Sleep(wait.Jitter(controllerCtx.ComponentConfig.Generic.ControllerStartInterval.Duration, ControllerStartJitter))\n   733→\n   734→\tlogger.V(1).Info(\"Starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   735→\n   736→\tinitFunc := controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n   737→\tctrl, started, err := initFunc(klog.NewContext(ctx, klog.LoggerWithName(logger, controllerName)), controllerCtx, controllerName)\n   738→\tif err != nil {\n   739→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   740→\t\treturn nil, err\n   741→\t}\n   742→\tif !started {\n   743→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: skipping controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   744→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   745→\t}\n   746→\n   747→\tcheck := controllerhealthz.NamedPingChecker(controllerName)\n   748→\tif ctrl != nil {\n   749→\t\t// check if the controller supports and requests a debugHandler\n   750→\t\t// and it needs the unsecuredMux to mount the handler onto.\n   751→\t\tif debuggable, ok := ctrl.(controller.Debuggable); ok && unsecuredMux != nil {\n   752→\t\t\tif debugHandler := debuggable.DebuggingHandler(); debugHandler != nil {\n   753→\t\t\t\tbasePath := \"/debug/controllers/\" + controllerName\n   754→\t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandle(basePath, http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n   755→\t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandlePrefix(basePath+\"/\", http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n   756→\t\t\t}\n   757→\t\t}\n   758→\t\tif healthCheckable, ok := ctrl.(controller.HealthCheckable); ok {\n   759→\t\t\tif realCheck := healthCheckable.HealthChecker(); realCheck != nil {\n   760→\t\t\t\tcheck = controllerhealthz.NamedHealthChecker(controllerName, realCheck)\n   761→\t\t\t}\n   762→\t\t}\n   763→\t}\n   764→\n   765→\tlogger.Info(\"Started controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   766→\treturn check, nil\n   767→}\n   768→\n   769→// err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcliflag.PrintFlags(cmd.Flags())\n\n\t\t\tc, err := s.Config(KnownControllers(), ControllersDisabledByDefault(), ControllerAliases())\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn s.ComponentGlobalsRegistry.FeatureGateFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent)\n\t\t\tfg.(featuregate.MutableFeatureGate).AddMetrics()\n\t\t\treturn Run(context.Background(), c.Complete())\n\t\t},\n\t\tArgs: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {\n\t\t\tfor _, arg := range args {\n\t\t\t\tif len(arg) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%q does not take any arguments, got %q\", cmd.CommandPath(), args)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tfs := cmd.Flags()\n\tnamedFlagSets := s.Flags(KnownControllers(), ControllersDisabledByDefault(), ControllerAliases())\n\tverflag.AddFlags(namedFlagSets.FlagSet(\"global\"))\n\tglobalflag.AddGlobalFlags(namedFlagSets.FlagSet(\"global\"), cmd.Name(), logs.SkipLoggingConfigurationFlags())\n\tfor _, f := range namedFlagSets.FlagSets {\n\t\tfs.AddFlagSet(f)\n\t}\n\n\tcols, _, _ := term.TerminalSize(cmd.OutOrStdout())\n\tcliflag.SetUsageAndHelpFunc(cmd, namedFlagSets, cols)\n\n\treturn cmd\n}\n\n// ResyncPeriod returns a function which generates a duration each time it is\n// invoked; this is so that multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all\n// hammer the apiserver with list requests simultaneously.\nfunc ResyncPeriod(c *config.CompletedConfig) func() time.Duration {\n\treturn func() time.Duration {\n\t\tfactor := rand.Float64() + 1\n\t\treturn time.Duration(float64(c.ComponentConfig.Generic.MinResyncPeriod.Nanoseconds()) * factor)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run runs the KubeControllerManagerOptions.\nfunc Run(ctx context.Context, c *config.CompletedConfig) error {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tstopCh := ctx.Done()\n\n\t// To help debugging, immediately log version\n\tlogger.Info(\"Starting\", \"version\", utilversion.Get())\n\n\tlogger.Info(\"Golang settings\", \"GOGC\", os.Getenv(\"GOGC\"), \"GOMAXPROCS\", os.Getenv(\"GOMAXPROCS\"), \"GOTRACEBACK\", os.Getenv(\"GOTRACEBACK\"))\n\n\t// Start events processing pipeline.\n\tc.EventBroadcaster.StartStructuredLogging(0)\n\tc.EventBroadcaster.StartRecordingToSink(&v1core.EventSinkImpl{Interface: c.Client.CoreV1().Events(\"\")})\n\tdefer c.EventBroadcaster.Shutdown()\n\n\tif cfgz, err := configz.New(ConfigzName); err == nil {\n\t\tcfgz.Set(c.ComponentConfig)\n\t} else {\n\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Unable to register configz\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Setup any healthz checks we will want to use.\n\tvar checks []healthz.HealthChecker\n\tvar electionChecker *leaderelection.HealthzAdaptor\n\tif c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.LeaderElect {\n\t\telectionChecker = leaderelection.NewLeaderHealthzAdaptor(time.Second * 20)\n\t\tchecks = append(checks, electionChecker)\n\t}\n\thealthzHandler := controllerhealthz.NewMutableHealthzHandler(checks...)\n\n\t// Start the controller manager HTTP server\n\t// unsecuredMux is the handler for these controller *after* authn/authz filters have been applied\n\tvar unsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux\n\tif c.SecureServing != nil {\n\t\tunsecuredMux = genericcontrollermanager.NewBaseHandler(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Debugging, healthzHandler)\n\t\tslis.SLIMetricsWithReset{}.Install(unsecuredMux)\n\n\t\thandler := genericcontrollermanager.BuildHandlerChain(unsecuredMux, &c.Authorization, &c.Authentication)\n\t\t// TODO: handle stoppedCh and listenerStoppedCh returned by c.SecureServing.Serve\n\t\tif _, _, err := c.SecureServing.Serve(handler, 0, stopCh); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tclientBuilder, rootClientBuilder := createClientBuilders(c)\n\n\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor := newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(rootClientBuilder)\n\n\trun := func(ctx context.Context, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor) {\n\t\tcontrollerContext, err := CreateControllerContext(ctx, c, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error building controller context\")\n\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err := StartControllers(ctx, controllerContext, controllerDescriptors, unsecuredMux, healthzHandler); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controllers\")\n\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n\t\tclose(controllerContext.InformersStarted)\n\n\t\t<-ctx.Done()\n\t}\n\n\t// No leader election, run directly\n\tif !c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.LeaderElect {\n\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tid, err := os.Hostname()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// add a uniquifier so that two processes on the same host don't accidentally both become active\n\tid = id + \"_\" + string(uuid.NewUUID())\n\n\t// leaderMigrator will be non-nil if and only if Leader Migration is enabled.\n\tvar leaderMigrator *leadermigration.LeaderMigrator = nil\n\n\t// If leader migration is enabled, create the LeaderMigrator and prepare for migration\n\tif leadermigration.Enabled(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic) {\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"starting leader migration\")\n\n\t\tleaderMigrator = leadermigration.NewLeaderMigrator(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration,\n\t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\")\n\n\t\t// startSATokenControllerInit is the original InitFunc.\n\t\tstartSATokenControllerInit := saTokenControllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n\n\t\t// Wrap saTokenControllerDescriptor to signal readiness for migration after starting\n\t\t//  the controller.\n\t\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor.initFunc = func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n\t\t\tdefer close(leaderMigrator.MigrationReady)\n\t\t\treturn startSATokenControllerInit(ctx, controllerContext, controllerName)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.CoordinatedLeaderElection) {\n\t\tbinaryVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).BinaryVersion().String())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\temulationVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).EmulationVersion().String())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Start lease candidate controller for coordinated leader election\n\t\tleaseCandidate, waitForSync, err := leaderelection.NewCandidate(\n\t\t\tc.Client,\n\t\t\t\"kube-system\",\n\t\t\tid,\n\t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\",\n\t\t\tbinaryVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n\t\t\temulationVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n\t\t\tcoordinationv1.OldestEmulationVersion,\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(healthz.NewInformerSyncHealthz(waitForSync))\n\n\t\tgo leaseCandidate.Run(ctx)\n\t}\n\n\t// Start the main lock\n\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceLock,\n\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceName,\n\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\t\t\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t// If leader migration is enabled, we should start only non-migrated controllers\n\t\t\t\t\t//  for the main lock.\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerNonMigrated)\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting main controllers.\")\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"leaderelection lost\")\n\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t})\n\n\t// If Leader Migration is enabled, proceed to attempt the migration lock.\n\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n\t\t// Wait for Service Account Token Controller to start before acquiring the migration lock.\n\t\t// At this point, the main lock must have already been acquired, or the KCM process already exited.\n\t\t// We wait for the main lock before acquiring the migration lock to prevent the situation\n\t\t//  where KCM instance A holds the main lock while KCM instance B holds the migration lock.\n\t\t<-leaderMigrator.MigrationReady\n\n\t\t// Start the migration lock.\n\t\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.ResourceLock,\n\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.LeaderName,\n\t\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n\t\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting migrated controllers.\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerMigrated)\n\t\t\t\t\t// DO NOT start saTokenController under migration lock\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(controllerDescriptors, names.ServiceAccountTokenController)\n\t\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"migration leaderelection lost\")\n\t\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\t<-stopCh\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\ntype ControllerContext struct {\n\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n\tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n\n\t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n\tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n\n\t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n\t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n\t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n\t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n\n\t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n\tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n\n\t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n\t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n\t// requested.\n\tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n\n\t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n\t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n\tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n\n\t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n\t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n\t// with list requests simultaneously.\n\tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n\n\t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n\tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n\n\t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n\tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n}\n\n// IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\nfunc (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n\tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n\t}\n\treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n}\n\n// InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n// that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n// can support the requested features.\n// The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n// that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n// Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n// The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\ntype InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n\ntype ControllerDescriptor struct {\n\tname                      string\n\tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n\trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n\taliases                   []string\n\tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n\tisCloudProviderController bool\n\trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n\treturn r.name\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n\treturn r.initFunc\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n\treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n}\n\n// GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n// Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n\treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n\treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsCloudProviderController() bool {\n\treturn r.isCloudProviderController\n}\n\n// RequiresSpecialHandling should return true only in a special non-generic controllers like ServiceAccountTokenController\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) RequiresSpecialHandling() bool {\n\treturn r.requiresSpecialHandling\n}\n\n// KnownControllers returns all known controllers's name\nfunc KnownControllers() []string {\n\treturn sets.StringKeySet(NewControllerDescriptors()).List()\n}\n\n// ControllerAliases returns a mapping of aliases to canonical controller names\nfunc ControllerAliases() map[string]string {\n\taliases := map[string]string{}\n\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n\t\tfor _, alias := range c.GetAliases() {\n\t\t\taliases[alias] = name\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn aliases\n}\n\nfunc ControllersDisabledByDefault() []string {\n\tvar controllersDisabledByDefault []string\n\n\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n\t\tif c.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n\t\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault = append(controllersDisabledByDefault, name)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tsort.Strings(controllersDisabledByDefault)\n\n\treturn controllersDisabledByDefault\n}\n\n// NewControllerDescriptors is a public map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n// paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n// This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\nfunc NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n\tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n\taliases := sets.NewString()\n\n\t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n\tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n\t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n\t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n\t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n\t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n\t\t}\n\t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n\t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n\t}\n\n\t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. These controllers cannot be initialized\n\t// in the main controller loop initialization, so we add them here only for the metadata and duplication detection.\n\t// app.ControllerDescriptor#RequiresSpecialHandling should return true for such controllers\n\t// The only known special case is the ServiceAccountTokenController which *must* be started\n\t// first to ensure that the SA tokens for future controllers will exist. Think very carefully before adding new\n\t// special controllers.\n\tregister(newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(nil))\n\n\tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNamespaceControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newServiceAccountControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newJobControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newReplicaSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newHorizontalPodAutoscalerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDisruptionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestApprovingControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTTLControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newBootstrapSignerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n\n\tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n\tregister(newNodeRouteControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n\tregister(newCloudNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor()) // cloud provider controller\n\t// TODO: persistent volume controllers into the IncludeCloudLoops only set as a cloud provider controller.\n\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeBinderControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeAttachDetachControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeExpanderControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newVolumeAttributesClassProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTTLAfterFinishedControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newRootCACertificatePublisherControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newKubeAPIServerSignerClusterTrustBundledPublisherDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEphemeralVolumeControllerDescriptor())\n\n\t// feature gated\n\tregister(newStorageVersionGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newResourceClaimControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newLegacyServiceAccountTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newValidatingAdmissionPolicyStatusControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTaintEvictionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newServiceCIDRsControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newStorageVersionMigratorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newSELinuxWarningControllerDescriptor())\n\n\tfor _, alias := range aliases.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tif _, ok := controllers[alias]; ok {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"alias %q conflicts with a controller name\", alias))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn controllers\n}\n\n// CreateControllerContext creates a context struct containing references to resources needed by the\n// controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n// the shared-informers client and token controller.\nfunc CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n\t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n\t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n\t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn obj, nil\n\t}\n\n\tversionedClient := rootClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\"shared-informers\")\n\tsharedInformers := informers.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(versionedClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), informers.WithTransform(trim))\n\n\tmetadataClient := metadata.NewForConfigOrDie(rootClientBuilder.ConfigOrDie(\"metadata-informers\"))\n\tmetadataInformers := metadatainformer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(metadataClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), metadatainformer.WithTransform(trim))\n\n\t// If apiserver is not running we should wait for some time and fail only then. This is particularly\n\t// important when we start apiserver and controller manager at the same time.\n\tif err := genericcontrollermanager.WaitForAPIServer(versionedClient, 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n\t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n\tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n\tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n\trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n\tgo wait.Until(func() {\n\t\trestMapper.Reset()\n\t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n\n\tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n\t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n\t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n\t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n\t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n\t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n\t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n\t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n\t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n\t}\n\n\tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector &&\n\t\tcontrollerContext.IsControllerEnabled(NewControllerDescriptors()[names.GarbageCollectorController]) {\n\t\tignoredResources := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n\t\tfor _, r := range controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.GCIgnoredResources {\n\t\t\tignoredResources[schema.GroupResource{Group: r.Group, Resource: r.Resource}] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollerContext.GraphBuilder = garbagecollector.NewDependencyGraphBuilder(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tmetadataClient,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.RESTMapper,\n\t\t\tignoredResources,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.InformersStarted,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tcontrollersmetrics.Register()\n\treturn controllerContext, nil\n}\n\n// StartControllers starts a set of controllers with a specified ControllerContext\nfunc StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n\n\t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n\t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n\tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif check != nil {\n\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n\t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n\t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n\t//\n\t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n\t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n\t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n\t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n\t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n\tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n\t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif check != nil {\n\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// StartController starts a controller with a specified ControllerContext\n// and performs required pre- and post- checks/actions\nfunc StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n\n\tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) 321→\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerNonMigrated)\n   322→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting main controllers.\")\n   323→\t\t\t\t}\n   324→\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n   325→\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n   326→\t\t\t},\n   327→\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n   328→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"leaderelection lost\")\n   329→\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n   330→\t\t\t},\n   331→\t\t})\n   332→\n   333→\t// If Leader Migration is enabled, proceed to attempt the migration lock.\n   334→\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n   335→\t\t// Wait for Service Account Token Controller to start before acquiring the migration lock.\n   336→\t\t// At this point, the main lock must have already been acquired, or the KCM process already exited.\n   337→\t\t// We wait for the main lock before acquiring the migration lock to prevent the situation\n   338→\t\t//  where KCM instance A holds the main lock while KCM instance B holds the migration lock.\n   339→\t\t<-leaderMigrator.MigrationReady\n   340→\n   341→\t\t// Start the migration lock.\n   342→\t\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n   343→\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.ResourceLock,\n   344→\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.LeaderName,\n   345→\t\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n   346→\t\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n   347→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting migrated controllers.\")\n   348→\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n   349→\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerMigrated)\n   350→\t\t\t\t\t// DO NOT start saTokenController under migration lock\n   351→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(controllerDescriptors, names.ServiceAccountTokenController)\n   352→\t\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n   353→\t\t\t\t},\n   354→\t\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n   355→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"migration leaderelection lost\")\n   356→\t\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n   357→\t\t\t\t},\n   358→\t\t\t})\n   359→\t}\n   360→\n   361→\t<-stopCh\n   362→\treturn nil\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→// ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\n   366→type ControllerContext struct {\n   367→\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n   368→\tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n   369→\n   370→\t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n   371→\tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n   372→\n   373→\t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n   374→\t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n   375→\t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n   376→\t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n   377→\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n   378→\n   379→\t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n   380→\tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n   381→\n   382→\t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n   383→\t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n   384→\t// requested.\n   385→\tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n   386→\n   387→\t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n   388→\t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n   389→\tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n   390→\n   391→\t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n   392→\t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n   393→\t// with list requests simultaneously.\n   394→\tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n   395→\n   396→\t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n   397→\tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n   398→\n   399→\t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n   400→\tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n   401→}\n   402→\n   403→// IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\n   404→func (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n   405→\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n   406→\tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n   407→\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n   408→\t}\n   409→\treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n   410→}\n   411→\n   412→// InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n   413→// that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n   414→// can support the requested features.\n   415→// The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n   416→// that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n   417→// Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n   418→// The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\n   419→type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n   420→\n   421→type ControllerDescriptor struct {\n   422→\tname                      string\n   423→\tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n   424→\trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n   425→\taliases                   []string\n   426→\tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n   427→\tisCloudProviderController bool\n   428→\trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n   429→}\n   430→\n   431→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n   432→\treturn r.name\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n   436→\treturn r.initFunc\n   437→}\n   438→\n   439→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n   440→\treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n   441→}\n   442→\n   443→// GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n   444→// Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\n   445→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n   446→\treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n   447→}\n   448→\n   449→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n   450→\treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n   451→}\n   452→\n   453→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsCloudProviderController() bool {\n   454→\treturn r.isCloudProviderController\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→// RequiresSpecialHandling should return true only in a special non-generic controllers like ServiceAccountTokenController\n   458→func (r *ControllerDescriptor) RequiresSpecialHandling() bool {\n   459→\treturn r.requiresSpecialHandling\n   460→}\n   461→\n   462→// KnownControllers returns all known controllers's name\n   463→func KnownControllers() []string {\n   464→\treturn sets.StringKeySet(NewControllerDescriptors()).List()\n   465→}\n   466→\n   467→// ControllerAliases returns a mapping of aliases to canonical controller names\n   468→func ControllerAliases() map[string]string {\n   469→\taliases := map[string]string{}\n   470→\tfor 477→\n   478→func ControllersDisabledByDefault() []string {\n   479→\tvar controllersDisabledByDefault []string\n   480→\n   481→\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n   482→\t\tif 487→\tsort.Strings(controllersDisabledByDefault)\n   488→\n   489→\treturn controllersDisabledByDefault\n   490→}\n   491→\n   492→// NewControllerDescriptors is a public map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n   493→// paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n   494→// This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\n   495→func NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n   496→\tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n   497→\taliases := sets.NewString()\n   498→\n   499→\t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n   500→\tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n   501→\t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n   502→\t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n   503→\t\t}\n   504→\t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n   505→\t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n   506→\t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n   507→\t\t}\n   508→\t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n   509→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n   512→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n   513→\t\t}\n   514→\n   515→\t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n   516→\t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n   517→\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n   518→\t\t\t}\n   519→\t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\n   522→\t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n   523→\t}\n   524→\n   525→\t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. These controllers cannot be initialized\n   526→\t// in the main controller loop initialization, so we add them here only for the metadata and duplication detection.\n   527→\t// app.ControllerDescriptor#RequiresSpecialHandling should return true for such controllers\n   528→\t// The only known special case is the ServiceAccountTokenController which *must* be started\n   529→\t// first to ensure that the SA tokens for future controllers will exist. Think very carefully before adding new\n   530→\t// special controllers.\n   531→\tregister(newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(nil))\n   532→\n   533→\tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n   534→\tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n   535→\tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n   536→\tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n   537→\tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   538→\tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n   539→\tregister(newNamespaceControllerDescriptor())\n   540→\tregister(newServiceAccountControllerDescriptor())\n   541→\tregister(newGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   542→\tregister(newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor())\n   543→\tregister(newJobControllerDescriptor())\n   544→\tregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\n   545→\tregister(newReplicaSetControllerDescriptor())\n   546→\tregister(newHorizontalPodAutoscalerControllerDescriptor())\n   547→\tregister(newDisruptionControllerDescriptor())\n   548→\tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n   549→\tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n   550→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n   551→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestApprovingControllerDescriptor())\n   552→\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   553→\tregister(newTTLControllerDescriptor())\n   554→\tregister(newBootstrapSignerControllerDescriptor())\n   555→\tregister(newTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   556→\tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n   557→\tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n   558→\n   559→\tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   560→\tregister(newNodeRouteControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   561→\tregister(newCloudNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor()) // cloud provider controller\n   562→\t// TODO: persistent volume controllers into the IncludeCloudLoops only set as a cloud provider controller.\n   563→\n   564→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeBinderControllerDescriptor())\n   565→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeAttachDetachControllerDescriptor())\n   566→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeExpanderControllerDescriptor())\n   567→\tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n   568→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   569→\tregister(newPersistentVolumeProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   570→\tregister(newVolumeAttributesClassProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   571→\tregister(newTTLAfterFinishedControllerDescriptor())\n   572→\tregister(newRootCACertificatePublisherControllerDescriptor())\n   573→\tregister(newKubeAPIServerSignerClusterTrustBundledPublisherDescriptor())\n   574→\tregister(newEphemeralVolumeControllerDescriptor())\n   575→\n   576→\t// feature gated\n   577→\tregister(newStorageVersionGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   578→\tregister(newResourceClaimControllerDescriptor())\n   579→\tregister(newLegacyServiceAccountTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n   580→\tregister(newValidatingAdmissionPolicyStatusControllerDescriptor())\n   581→\tregister(newTaintEvictionControllerDescriptor())\n   582→\tregister(newServiceCIDRsControllerDescriptor())\n   583→\tregister(newStorageVersionMigratorControllerDescriptor())\n   584→\tregister(newSELinuxWarningControllerDescriptor())\n   585→\n   586→\tfor _, alias := range aliases.UnsortedList() {\n   587→\t\tif _, ok := controllers[alias]; ok {\n   588→\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"alias %q conflicts with a controller name\", alias))\n   589→\t\t}\n   590→\t}\n   591→\n   592→\treturn controllers\n   593→}\n   594→\n   595→// CreateControllerContext creates a context struct containing references to resources needed by the\n   596→// controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n   597→// the shared-informers client and token controller.\n   598→func CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n   599→\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n   600→\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n   601→\t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n   602→\t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n   603→\t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n   604→\t\t\t}\n   605→\t\t}\n   606→\t\treturn obj, nil\n   607→\t}\n   608→\n   609→\tversionedClient := rootClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\"shared-informers\")\n   610→\tsharedInformers := informers.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(versionedClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), informers.WithTransform(trim))\n   611→\n   612→\tmetadataClient := metadata.NewForConfigOrDie(rootClientBuilder.ConfigOrDie(\"metadata-informers\"))\n   613→\tmetadataInformers := metadatainformer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(metadataClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), metadatainformer.WithTransform(trim))\n   614→\n   615→\t// If apiserver is not running we should wait for some time and fail only then. This is particularly\n   616→\t// important when we start apiserver and controller manager at the same time.\n   617→\tif err := genericcontrollermanager.WaitForAPIServer(versionedClient, 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n   619→\t}\n   620→\n   621→\t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n   622→\tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n   623→\tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n   624→\trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n   625→\tgo wait.Until(func() {\n   626→\t\trestMapper.Reset()\n   627→\t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n   628→\n   629→\tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n   630→\t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n   631→\t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n   632→\t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n   633→\t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n   634→\t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n   635→\t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n   636→\t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n   637→\t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n   638→\t}\n   639→\n   640→\tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector &&\n   641→\t\tcontrollerContext.IsControllerEnabled(NewControllerDescriptors()[names.GarbageCollectorController]) {\n   642→\t\tignoredResources := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n   643→\t\tfor _, r := range controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.GCIgnoredResources {\n   644→\t\t\tignoredResources[schema.GroupResource{Group: r.Group, Resource: r.Resource}] = struct{}{}\n   645→\t\t}\n   646→\n   647→\t\tcontrollerContext.GraphBuilder = garbagecollector.NewDependencyGraphBuilder(\n   648→\t\t\tctx,\n   649→\t\t\tmetadataClient,\n   650→\t\t\tcontrollerContext.RESTMapper,\n   651→\t\t\tignoredResources,\n   652→\t\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory,\n   653→\t\t\tcontrollerContext.InformersStarted,\n   654→\t\t)\n   655→\t}\n   656→\n   657→\tcontrollersmetrics.Register()\n   658→\treturn controllerContext, nil\n   659→}\n   660→\n   661→// StartControllers starts a set of controllers with a specified ControllerContext\n   662→func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n   663→\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n   664→\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n   665→\n   666→\t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n   667→\t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n   668→\tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n   669→\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n   670→\t\tif err != nil {\n   671→\t\t\treturn err\n   672→\t\t}\n   673→\t\tif check != nil {\n   674→\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n   675→\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n   676→\t\t}\n   677→\t}\n   678→\n   679→\t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n   680→\t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n   681→\t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n   682→\t//\n   683→\t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n   684→\t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n   685→\t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n   686→\t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n   687→\t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n   688→\tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n   689→\t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n   690→\t\t\tcontinue\n   691→\t\t}\n   692→\n   693→\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n   694→\t\tif err != nil {\n   695→\t\t\treturn err\n   696→\t\t}\n   697→\t\tif check != nil {\n   698→\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n   699→\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n   700→\t\t}\n   701→\t}\n   702→\n   703→\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n   704→\n   705→\treturn nil\n   706→}\n   707→\n   708→// StartController starts a controller with a specified ControllerContext\n   709→// and performs required pre- and post- checks/actions\n   710→func StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n   711→\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n   712→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   713→\tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n   714→\n   715→\tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n   716→\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) {\n   717→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Controller is disabled by a feature gate\", \"controller\", controllerName, \"requiredFeatureGates\", controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates())\n   718→\t\t\treturn nil, nil\n   719→\t\t}\n   720→\t}\n   721→\n   722→\tif controllerDescriptor.IsCloudProviderController() {\n   723→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping a cloud provider controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   724→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   725→\t}\n   726→\n   727→\tif !controllerCtx.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor) {\n   728→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: controller is disabled\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   729→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   730→\t}\n   731→\n   732→\ttime.Sleep(wait.Jitter(controllerCtx.ComponentConfig.Generic.ControllerStartInterval.Duration, ControllerStartJitter))\n   733→\n   734→\tlogger.V(1).Info(\"Starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   735→\n   736→\tinitFunc := controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n   737→\tctrl, started, err := initFunc(klog.NewContext(ctx, klog.LoggerWithName(logger, controllerName)), controllerCtx, controllerName)\n   738→\tif err != nil {\n   739→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   740→\t\treturn nil, err\n   741→\t}\n   742→\tif !started {\n   743→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: skipping controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   744→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   745→\t}\n   746→\n   747→\tcheck := controllerhealthz.NamedPingChecker(controllerName)\n   748→\tif ctrl != nil {\n   749→\t\t// check if the controller supports and requests a debugHandler\n   750→\t\t// and it needs the unsecuredMux to mount the handler onto.\n   751→\t\tif debuggable, ok := ctrl.(controller.Debuggable); ok && unsecuredMux != nil {\n   752→\t\t\tif debugHandler := debuggable.DebuggingHandler(); debugHandler != nil {\n   753→\t\t\t\tbasePath := \"/debug/controllers/\" + controllerName\n   754→\t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandle(basePath, http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n   755→\t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandlePrefix(basePath+\"/\", http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n   756→\t\t\t}\n   757→\t\t}\n   758→\t\tif healthCheckable, ok := ctrl.(controller.HealthCheckable); ok {\n   759→\t\t\tif realCheck := healthCheckable.HealthChecker(); realCheck != nil {\n   760→\t\t\t\tcheck = controllerhealthz.NamedHealthChecker(controllerName, realCheck)\n   761→\t\t\t}\n   762→\t\t}\n   763→\t}\n   764→\n   765→\tlogger.Info(\"Started controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n   766→\treturn check, nil\n   767→}\n   768→\n   769→// serviceAccountTokenControllerStarter is special because it must run first to set up permissions for other controllers.\n   770→// It cannot use the \"normal\" client builder, so it tracks its own.\n   771→func newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(rootClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) *ControllerDescriptor {\n   772→\treturn &ControllerDescriptor{\n   773→\t\tname:    names.ServiceAccountTokenController,\n   774→\t\taliases: []string{\"serviceaccount-token\"},\n   775→\t\tinitFunc: func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n   776→\t\t\treturn startServiceAccountTokenController(ctx, controllerContext, controllerName, rootClientBuilder)\n   777→\t\t},\n   778→\t\t// will make sure it runs first before other controllers\n   779→\t\trequiresSpecialHandling: true,\n   780→\t}\n   781→}\n   782→\n   783→func startServiceAccountTokenController(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string, rootClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n   784→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   785→\tif len(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.SAController.ServiceAccountKeyFile) == 0 {\n   786→\t\tlogger.Info(\"Controller is disabled because there is no private key\", \"controller\",
